<pr_description>
MudDataGrid needs a SortChanged event that can be subscribed to.
### Feature request type

Enhance component

### Component name

MudDataGrid

### Is your feature request related to a problem?

No

### Describe the solution you'd like

Currently, there is no way to easily tell when the sort has changed in the data grid. There is a SortDefinitions parameter but the type is an Dictionary<string, SortDefinition> which does not allow notifying when a definition has been added, removed or changed. There needs to be an event, SortChanged than can be subscribed to for notifying when the sort of the data grid has changed.

### Have you seen this feature anywhere else?

No

### Describe alternatives you've considered

The only solution really is implementing your own ObservableDictionary.

- [ ] I would like to do a Pull Request

   219	        private static void Swap<TItem>(List<TItem> list, int indexA, int indexB)
   220	        {
   221	            (list[indexB], list[indexA]) = (list[indexA], list[indexB]);
   222	        }

   224	        private Task ItemUpdatedAsync(MudItemDropInfo<Column<T>> dropItem)
   225	        {
   226	            Debug.Assert(dropItem.Item is not null);
   227	            dropItem.Item.Identifier = dropItem.DropzoneIdentifier;
   228	
   229	            var dragAndDropSource = RenderedColumns.SingleOrDefault(rc => rc.PropertyName == dropItem.Item?.PropertyName);
   230	            var dragAndDropDestination = RenderedColumns.SingleOrDefault(rc => rc.PropertyName == dropItem.DropzoneIdentifier);
   231	            if (dragAndDropSource != null && dragAndDropDestination != null)
   232	            {
   233	                var dragAndDropSourceIndex = RenderedColumns.IndexOf(dragAndDropSource);
   234	                var dragAndDropDestinationIndex = RenderedColumns.IndexOf(dragAndDropDestination);
   235	
   236	                Swap(RenderedColumns, dragAndDropSourceIndex, dragAndDropDestinationIndex);
   237	
   238	                Debug.Assert(dragAndDropSource.HeaderCell is not null);
   239	                Debug.Assert(dragAndDropDestination.HeaderCell is not null);
   240	
   241	                // swap source / destination
   242	                var dest = dragAndDropDestination.HeaderCell.Width;
   243	                var src = dragAndDropSource.HeaderCell.Width;
   244	
   245	                dragAndDropSource.HeaderCell.Width = dest;
   246	                dragAndDropDestination.HeaderCell.Width = src;
   247	
   248	                StateHasChanged();
   249	            }
   250	            return Task.CompletedTask;
   251	        }

   495	        /// </remarks>

   497	        public Breakpoint Breakpoint { get; set; } = Breakpoint.Xs;
   498

   784	        /// </remarks>

   787	
   788	        /// <summary>
   789	        /// The data for this grid when <see cref="ServerData"/> is not set.
   790	        /// </summary>
   791	        /// <remarks>
   792	        /// One row will be displayed per item.  Use the <see cref="ServerData"/> function instead of this property to get data on demand.
   793	        /// </remarks>
   794	        [Parameter, ParameterState(ParameterUsage = ParameterUsageOptions.None)]
   795	        public IEnumerable<T>? Items { get; set; }
   796	
   797	        private void OnPagerStateChanged()
   798	        {
   799	            if (PagerStateHasChangedEvent is not null)
   800	                InvokeAsync(PagerStateHasChangedEvent);
   801	        }
   802	
   803	        private void SetupGrouping()
   804	        {
   805	            if (Groupable)
   806	                GroupItems();
   807	        }
   808	
   809	        private void SetupCollectionChangeTracking()
   810	        {
   811	            if (Items is INotifyCollectionChanged changed)
   812	            {
   813	                changed.CollectionChanged += (s, e) =>
   814	                {
   815	                    InvokeAsync(async () =>
   816	                    {
   817	                        _currentRenderFilteredItemsCache = null;
   818	
   819	                        if (Groupable)
   820	                            GroupItems();
   821	
   822	                        ApplyInitialExpansionForNewItems(e);
   823	                        await CleanupRemovedItemsAsync(e);
   824	                        StateHasChanged();
   825	                    });
   826	                };
   827	            }
   828	        }
   829	
   830	        private async Task CleanupRemovedItemsAsync(NotifyCollectionChangedEventArgs e)
   831	        {
   832	            if (e.Action == NotifyCollectionChangedAction.Reset)
   833	            {
   834	                // For reset, check all items in selection against the current items
   835	                await CleanupStaleSelectionsAsync();
   836	                CleanupStaleHierarchyExpansions();
   837	                return;
   838	            }
   839	
   840	            if (e.OldItems is null)
   841	                return;
   842	
   843	            // Build a set of removed items for efficient lookup
   844	            var removedItems = new HashSet<T>(e.OldItems.Cast<T>(), Comparer);
   845	
   846	            // Directly check removed items against selection (more efficient for small removals)
   847	            var (selectionChanged, selectedItemChanged) = PruneSelectionFromRemovedItems(removedItems);
   848	
   849	            // Handle SelectedItem reset if needed
   850	            if (selectedItemChanged)
   851	            {
   852	                await _selectedItemState.SetValueAsync(default);
   853	            }
   854	
   855	            // Clean up hierarchy expansions for removed items
   856	            PruneHierarchyExpansions(removedItems);
   857	
   858	            if (selectionChanged)
   859	            {
   860	                await FireSelectionChangedEventsAsync();
   861	            }
   862	        }
   863	
   864	        private async Task CleanupStaleSelectionsAsync()
   865	        {
   866	            if (Selection.Count == 0 && _selectedItemState.Value is null)
   867	                return;
   868	
   869	            var currentItems = BuildCurrentItemsSet();
   870	            var (selectionChanged, selectedItemChanged) = PruneSelectionAndSelectedItem(currentItems);
   871	
   872	            if (!selectionChanged && !selectedItemChanged)
   873	                return;
   874	
   875	            if (selectedItemChanged)
   876	            {
   877	                await _selectedItemState.SetValueAsync(default);
   878	            }
   879	
   880	            if (selectionChanged)
   881	            {
   882	                await FireSelectionChangedEventsAsync();
   883	            }
   884	        }
   885	
   886	        private void CleanupStaleHierarchyExpansions()
   887	        {
   888	            if (_openHierarchies.Count == 0 && _initialExpansions.Count == 0)
   889	                return;
   890	
   891	            var currentItems = BuildCurrentItemsSet();
   892	            PruneHierarchyExpansionsFromCurrentItems(currentItems);
   893	        }
   894	
   895	        /// <summary>
   896	        /// Builds a HashSet of current items from the data source.
   897	        /// </summary>
   898	        private HashSet<T> BuildCurrentItemsSet()
   899	        {
   900	            return Items is not null ? new HashSet<T>(Items, Comparer) : new HashSet<T>(Comparer);
   901	        }
   902	
   903	        /// <summary>
   904	        /// Removes items from Selection that are not present in currentItems.
   905	        /// Returns a tuple indicating whether Selection changed and whether SelectedItem needs to be reset.
   906	        /// </summary>
   907	        private (bool SelectionChanged, bool SelectedItemChanged) PruneSelectionAndSelectedItem(HashSet<T> currentItems)
   908	        {
   909	            var selectionChanged = Selection.RemoveWhere(s => !currentItems.Contains(s)) > 0;
   910	
   911	            // Check if SelectedItem needs to be reset
   912	            var selectedItemChanged = _selectedItemState.Value is not null && !currentItems.Contains(_selectedItemState.Value);
   913	
   914	            return (selectionChanged, selectedItemChanged);
   915	        }
   916	
   917	        /// <summary>
   918	        /// Removes items from Selection that are present in removedItems.
   919	        /// More efficient when a small number of items are removed from a large collection.
   920	        /// </summary>
   921	        private (bool SelectionChanged, bool SelectedItemChanged) PruneSelectionFromRemovedItems(HashSet<T> removedItems)
   922	        {
   923	            var selectionChanged = false;
   924	            foreach (var item in removedItems)
   925	            {
   926	                if (Selection.Remove(item))
   927	                {
   928	                    selectionChanged = true;
   929	                }
   930	            }
   931	
   932	            // Check if SelectedItem needs to be reset
   933	            var selectedItemChanged = _selectedItemState.Value is not null && removedItems.Contains(_selectedItemState.Value);
   934	
   935	            return (selectionChanged, selectedItemChanged);
   936	        }
   937	
   938	        /// <summary>
   939	        /// Removes items from _openHierarchies and _initialExpansions that are present in the removedItems set.
   940	        /// Used when specific items are removed from the collection.
   941	        /// </summary>
   942	        private void PruneHierarchyExpansions(HashSet<T> removedItems)
   943	        {
   944	            _openHierarchies.ExceptWith(removedItems);
   945	            _initialExpansions.ExceptWith(removedItems);
   946	        }
   947	
   948	        /// <summary>
   949	        /// Removes items from _openHierarchies and _initialExpansions that are not present in currentItems.
   950	        /// Used when checking against the full current items set.
   951	        /// </summary>
   952	        private void PruneHierarchyExpansionsFromCurrentItems(HashSet<T> currentItems)
   953	        {
   954	            _openHierarchies.RemoveWhere(h => !currentItems.Contains(h));
   955	            _initialExpansions.RemoveWhere(e => !currentItems.Contains(e));
   956	        }
   957	
   958	        /// <summary>
   959	        /// Fires SelectedItemsChanged event and invokes SelectedItemsChangedEvent.
   960	        /// </summary>
   961	        private async Task FireSelectionChangedEventsAsync()
   962	        {
   963	            // Create new HashSet instance to ensure ParameterState's comparer detects changes
   964	            await _selectedItemsState.SetValueAsync(new HashSet<T>(Selection, Comparer));
   965	            SelectedItemsChangedEvent?.Invoke(Selection);
   966	        }
   967	
   968	        private void ApplyInitialExpansionForNewItems(NotifyCollectionChangedEventArgs e)
   969	        {
   970	            if (_initialExpandedFunc is null || e.NewItems is null)
   971	                return;
   972	
   973	            foreach (T item in e.NewItems)
   974	            {
   975	                if (_initialExpandedFunc.Invoke(item) && _initialExpansions.Add(item))
   976	                {
   977	                    _openHierarchies.Add(item);
   978	                }
   979	            }
   980	        }
   981	
   982	        private void ApplyInitialExpansionForItems(IEnumerable<T>? items)
   983	        {
   984	            if (_initialExpandedFunc is null || items is null)
   985	                return;
   986	
   987	            foreach (var item in items)
   988	            {
   989	                if (_initialExpandedFunc.Invoke(item) && _initialExpansions.Add(item))
   990	                {
   991	                    _openHierarchies.Add(item);
   992	                }
   993	            }
   994	        }
   995

  1082

  1198	                _currentPage = value;
  1199	                InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);

  1203	                    InvokeAsync(InvokeServerLoadFunc);

  1359	        internal IEnumerable<T> CurrentPageItems
  1360	        {
  1361	            get
  1362	            {
  1363	                if (PagerContent == null)
  1364	                {
  1365	                    return FilteredItems; // we have no pagination
  1366	                }
  1367	
  1368	                if (!HasServerData)
  1369	                {
  1370	                    var filteredItemCount = GetFilteredItemsCount();
  1371	                    int lastPageNo;
  1372	                    if (filteredItemCount == 0)
  1373	                        lastPageNo = 0;
  1374	                    else
  1375	                        lastPageNo = (filteredItemCount / RowsPerPage) - (filteredItemCount % RowsPerPage == 0 ? 1 : 0);
  1376	                    CurrentPage = lastPageNo < CurrentPage ? lastPageNo : CurrentPage;
  1377	                }
  1378	
  1379	                return GetItemsOfPage(CurrentPage, RowsPerPage);
  1380	            }
  1381	        }
  1382	
  1383	        /// <summary>
  1384	        /// The currently selected items.
  1385	        /// </summary>
  1386	        public HashSet<T> Selection { get; set; }

  1391	        public bool HasPager { get; set; }

  1397	
  1398	        /// <summary>
  1399	        /// Defines the ItemsProviderDelegate property, which is necessary for implementing the ServerData methodology with Virtualization.
  1400	        /// This property is used to populate items virtually from the server.
  1401	        /// </summary>
  1402	        internal ItemsProviderDelegate<IndexBag<T>>? VirtualItemsProvider { get; set; }
  1403	
  1404	        /// <summary>
  1405	        /// For unit testing the filtering cache mechanism.
  1406	        /// </summary>
  1407	        internal uint FilteringRunCount { get; private set; }
  1408	
  1409	        /// <summary>
  1410	        /// The items which remain after applying filters.
  1411	        /// </summary>
  1412	        public IEnumerable<T> FilteredItems
  1413	        {
  1414	            // TODO: When adding one FilterDefinition, this is called once for each RenderedColumn...
  1415	            get
  1416	            {
  1417	                if (_currentRenderFilteredItemsCache != null) return _currentRenderFilteredItemsCache;
  1418	                var items = HasServerData
  1419	                    ? _serverData.Items
  1420	                    : Items;
  1421	
  1422	                items ??= Enumerable.Empty<T>();
  1423	
  1424	                // Quick filtering
  1425	                if (QuickFilter != null)
  1426	                {
  1427	                    items = items.Where(QuickFilter);
  1428	                }
  1429	
  1430	                if (!HasServerData)
  1431	                {
  1432	                    foreach (var filterDefinition in FilterDefinitions)
  1433	                    {
  1434	                        var filterFunc = filterDefinition.GenerateFilterFunction(new FilterOptions
  1435	                        {
  1436	                            FilterCaseSensitivity = FilterCaseSensitivity
  1437	                        });
  1438	                        items = items.Where(filterFunc);
  1439	                    }
  1440	                }
  1441	
  1442	                _currentRenderFilteredItemsCache = Sort(items).ToList(); // To list to ensure evaluation only once per render
  1443	                unchecked { FilteringRunCount++; }
  1444	                GroupItems(noStateChange: true);
  1445	                return _currentRenderFilteredItemsCache;
  1446	            }
  1447	        }
  1448	
  1449	        /// <summary>
  1450	        /// The validator which validates values in each row.
  1451	        /// </summary>
  1452	        /// <remarks>
  1453	        /// Use to bind validation and touched handling to outer form.
  1454	        /// </remarks>
  1455	        [Parameter]
  1456	        public Interfaces.IForm Validator { get; set; } = new DataGridRowValidator();

  1473	        internal string GetGroupIcon(bool isExpanded, bool? rtl = null)

  1475	            if (rtl == null)
  1476	                rtl = RightToLeft;
  1477	            if (isExpanded)
  1478	            {
  1479	                return Icons.Material.Filled.ExpandMore;
  1480	            }
  1481	            return rtl.Value ? Icons.Material.Filled.ChevronLeft : Icons.Material.Filled.ChevronRight;
  1482	        }

  1508	        /// <summary>
  1509	        /// This property is determined by checking if the <see cref="ServerData"/> or <see cref="VirtualizeServerData"/> property is not null.
  1510	        /// </summary>
  1511	        internal bool HasServerData => ServerData != null || VirtualizeServerData != null;

  1513	        #endregion
  1514	
  1515	        protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
  1516	        {
  1517	            if (firstRender)
  1518	            {
  1519	                await InvokeServerLoadFunc();
  1520	                if (HasServerData)
  1521	                    StateHasChanged();
  1522	                _isFirstRendered = true;
  1523	            }
  1524	            else
  1525	            {
  1526	                PagerStateHasChangedEvent?.Invoke();
  1527	            }
  1528	
  1529	            await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);
  1530	        }
  1531	
  1532	        public override async Task SetParametersAsync(ParameterView parameters)
  1533	        {
  1534	            var sortModeBefore = SortMode;
  1535	            await base.SetParametersAsync(parameters);
  1536	
  1537	            VirtualItemsProviderInitialize();
  1538	            if (parameters.TryGetValue(nameof(SortMode), out SortMode sortMode) && sortMode != sortModeBefore)
  1539	                await ClearCurrentSortings();
  1540	        }
  1541	
  1542	        private async Task OnItemsChangedAsync(ParameterChangedEventArgs<IEnumerable<T>?> args)
  1543	        {
  1544	            // Always clean up stale selections when Items is reassigned.
  1545	            // For INotifyCollectionChanged (e.g., ObservableCollection), the event handler
  1546	            // additionally handles incremental changes (add/remove without reassigning).
  1547	            await CleanupStaleSelectionsAsync();
  1548	            CleanupStaleHierarchyExpansions();
  1549	
  1550	            OnPagerStateChanged();
  1551	            SetupGrouping();
  1552	            ApplyInitialExpansionForItems(args.Value);
  1553	            SetupCollectionChangeTracking();
  1554	        }
  1555	
  1556	        private async Task OnSelectedItemChangedAsync(ParameterChangedEventArgs<T?> args)
  1557	        {
  1558	            if (args.Value is null)
  1559	            {
  1560	                return;
  1561	            }
  1562	
  1563	            if (!MultiSelection)
  1564	            {
  1565	                Selection.Clear();
  1566	            }
  1567	
  1568	            // add new item to Selection
  1569	            if (!Selection.Remove(args.Value))
  1570	            {
  1571	                Selection.Add(args.Value);
  1572	            }
  1573	
  1574	            // Create new HashSet instance to ensure ParameterState's comparer detects changes
  1575	            await _selectedItemsState.SetValueAsync(new HashSet<T>(Selection, Comparer));
  1576	        }
  1577	
  1578	        private void OnSelectedItemsChanged(ParameterChangedEventArgs<HashSet<T>?> args)
  1579	        {
  1580	            // Make defensive copy to avoid shared references between parent and child
  1581	            if (args.Value == null)
  1582	            {
  1583	                Selection.Clear();
  1584	            }
  1585	            else
  1586	            {
  1587	                Selection.Clear();
  1588	                Selection.UnionWith(args.Value);
  1589	            }
  1590	        }
  1591	
  1592	        private async Task OnExpandSingleRowChangedAsync(ParameterChangedEventArgs<bool> args)
  1593	        {
  1594	            // If user changes the ExpandSingleRow parameter, clear all open hierarchies except the first
  1595	            if (_openHierarchies.Count > 0)
  1596	            {
  1597	                var first = _openHierarchies.First();
  1598	                foreach (var item in _openHierarchies.Skip(1))
  1599	                {
  1600	                    await HierarchyVisibilityToggled.InvokeAsync(new(item, false));
  1601	                }
  1602	                _openHierarchies.Clear();
  1603	                _openHierarchies.Add(first);
  1604	                await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
  1605	            }
  1606	        }
  1607	
  1608	        /// <summary>
  1609	        /// Check if a specific Footer cell is displayable
  1610	        /// </summary>
  1611	        /// <param name="column"></param>
  1612	        /// <returns><see langword="true"/> when the cell can be displayed</returns>
  1613	        private static bool IsFooterCellDisplayable(Column<T> column)
  1614	        {
  1615	            return !column.HiddenState.Value && (column.GetFooterTemplate() != null || column.AggregateDefinition != null);
  1616	        }
  1617	
  1618	        protected IEnumerable<T> GetItemsOfPage(int page, int pageSize)
  1619	        {
  1620	            if (page < 0 || pageSize <= 0)
  1621	                return Array.Empty<T>();
  1622	
  1623	            if (HasServerData)
  1624	            {
  1625	                return _serverData.Items;
  1626	            }
  1627	
  1628	            return FilteredItems.Skip(page * pageSize).Take(pageSize);
  1629	        }
  1630	
  1631	        internal async Task InvokeServerLoadFunc()
  1632	        {
  1633	            if (!HasServerData)
  1634	                return;
  1635	
  1636	            if (VirtualizeServerData != null)
  1637	            {
  1638	                if (_mudVirtualize != null)
  1639	                {
  1640	                    // Cancel any prior request
  1641	                    CancelServerDataToken();
  1642	                    await _mudVirtualize.RefreshDataAsync();
  1643	                }
  1644	                else
  1645	                {
  1646	                    Loading = true;
  1647	                    StateHasChanged();
  1648	
  1649	                    var state = new GridStateVirtualize<T>
  1650	                    {
  1651	                        StartIndex = 0,
  1652	                        Count = 1,
  1653	                        SortDefinitions = SortDefinitions.Values.OrderBy(sd => sd.Index).ToList(),
  1654	                        // Additional ToList() here to decouple clients from internal list avoiding runtime issues
  1655	                        FilterDefinitions = FilterDefinitions.ToList()
  1656	                    };
  1657	
  1658	                    // Cancel any prior request
  1659	                    CancelServerDataToken();
  1660	
  1661	                    Debug.Assert(_serverDataCancellationTokenSource is not null);
  1662	                    _serverData = await VirtualizeServerData(state, _serverDataCancellationTokenSource.Token);
  1663	                    _currentRenderFilteredItemsCache = null;
  1664	
  1665	                    Loading = false;
  1666	                }
  1667	            }
  1668	            else
  1669	            {
  1670	                Loading = true;
  1671	                StateHasChanged();
  1672	
  1673	                var state = new GridState<T>
  1674	                {
  1675	                    Page = CurrentPage,
  1676	                    PageSize = RowsPerPage,
  1677	                    SortDefinitions = SortDefinitions.Values.OrderBy(sd => sd.Index).ToList(),
  1678	                    // Additional ToList() here to decouple clients from internal list avoiding runtime issues
  1679	                    FilterDefinitions = FilterDefinitions.ToList()
  1680	                };
  1681	
  1682	                // Cancel any prior request
  1683	                CancelServerDataToken();
  1684	
  1685	                Debug.Assert(ServerData is not null);
  1686	                Debug.Assert(_serverDataCancellationTokenSource is not null);
  1687	                _serverData = await ServerData(state, _serverDataCancellationTokenSource.Token);
  1688	                _currentRenderFilteredItemsCache = null;
  1689	
  1690	                if (CurrentPage * RowsPerPage > _serverData.TotalItems)
  1691	                    CurrentPage = 0;
  1692	
  1693	                Loading = false;
  1694	                PagerStateHasChangedEvent?.Invoke();
  1695	            }
  1696	            // handle initial hierarchy expansion
  1697	            if (_initialExpandedFunc is not null)
  1698	            {
  1699	                foreach (var data in _serverData.Items)
  1700	                {
  1701	                    // ensure we only add it once if they were expanded initially
  1702	                    if (_initialExpandedFunc(data) && _initialExpansions.Add(data))
  1703	                    {
  1704	                        _openHierarchies.Add(data);
  1705	                    }
  1706	                }
  1707	            }
  1708	
  1709	            StateHasChanged();
  1710	            GroupItems();
  1711	        }
  1712	
  1713	        internal void AddColumn(Column<T> column)
  1714	        {
  1715	            if (column.Tag?.ToString() == "hierarchy-column")
  1716	            {
  1717	                if (column is TemplateColumn<T> templateColumn)
  1718	                {
  1719	                    _initialExpandedFunc = templateColumn.InitiallyExpandedFunc;
  1720	                    _buttonDisabledFunc = templateColumn.ButtonDisabledFunc;
  1721	                    // Apply expansion now if items or _serverData.Items is already set
  1722	                    if (Items is not null)
  1723	                    {
  1724	                        ApplyInitialExpansionForItems(Items);
  1725	                    }
  1726	                    else if (_serverData?.Items?.Any() == true)
  1727	                    {
  1728	                        ApplyInitialExpansionForItems(_serverData.Items);
  1729	                    }
  1730	                }
  1731	                RenderedColumns.Insert(0, column);
  1732	            }
  1733	            else if (column.Tag?.ToString() == "select-column")
  1734	            {
  1735	                // Position SelectColumn after HierarchyColumn if present
  1736	                if (RenderedColumns.Select(x => x.Tag).Contains("hierarchy-column"))
  1737	                {
  1738	                    RenderedColumns.Insert(1, column);
  1739	                }
  1740	                else
  1741	                {
  1742	                    RenderedColumns.Insert(0, column);
  1743	                }
  1744	            }
  1745	            else
  1746	            {
  1747	                RenderedColumns.Add(column);
  1748	            }
  1749	        }
  1750	
  1751	        internal void CancelServerDataToken()
  1752	        {
  1753	            try
  1754	            {
  1755	                _serverDataCancellationTokenSource?.Cancel();
  1756	                _serverDataCancellationTokenSource?.Dispose();
  1757	            }
  1758	            catch { /*ignored*/ }
  1759	            finally
  1760	            {
  1761	                _serverDataCancellationTokenSource = new CancellationTokenSource();
  1762	            }
  1763	        }
  1764	
  1765	        internal void RemoveColumn(Column<T> column)
  1766	        {
  1767	            RenderedColumns.Remove(column);
  1768	        }
  1769	
  1770	        internal IFilterDefinition<T> CreateFilterDefinitionInstance()
  1771	        {
  1772	            return _defaultFilterDefinitionFactory();
  1773	        }
  1774	
  1775	        /// <summary>
  1776	        /// Creates a <see cref="FilterContext{T}"/> for a specific <see cref="IFilterDefinition{T}"/>,
  1777	        /// allowing each filter row to have its own independent context instance.
  1778	        /// </summary>
  1779	        /// <param name="column">The column associated with the filter.</param>
  1780	        /// <param name="filterDefinition">The filter definition for this context.</param>
  1781	        /// <returns>A new <see cref="FilterContext{T}"/> bound to the specified filter definition.</returns>
  1782	        internal FilterContext<T> CreateFilterContext(Column<T> column, IFilterDefinition<T> filterDefinition)
  1783	        {
  1784	            var context = new FilterContext<T>(this)
  1785	            {
  1786	                FilterDefinition = filterDefinition,
  1787	                HeaderCell = column.FilterContext.HeaderCell
  1788	            };
  1789	            context.SetActions(new FilterContext<T>.FilterActions
  1790	            {
  1791	                ApplyFilterAsync = ApplyFilterFromSimpleModeAsync,
  1792	                ApplyFiltersAsync = ApplyFiltersFromSimpleModeAsync,
  1793	                ClearFilterAsync = ClearFilterFromSimpleModeAsync,
  1794	                ClearFiltersAsync = ClearFiltersFromSimpleModeAsync,
  1795	                CloseFilterAsync = CloseFilterAsync
  1796	            });
  1797	
  1798	            return context;
  1799	        }
  1800	
  1801	        private async Task ApplyFilterFromSimpleModeAsync(IFilterDefinition<T> filterDefinition)
  1802	        {
  1803	            if (FilterDefinitions.All(x => x.Id != filterDefinition.Id))
  1804	            {
  1805	                FilterDefinitions.Add(filterDefinition);
  1806	            }
  1807	
  1808	            await InvokeServerLoadFunc();
  1809	            GroupItems();
  1810	            await NotifyFilterChangedAsync();
  1811	
  1812	            if (!HasServerData)
  1813	            {
  1814	                StateHasChanged();
  1815	            }
  1816	        }
  1817	
  1818	        private async Task ApplyFiltersFromSimpleModeAsync(IEnumerable<IFilterDefinition<T>> filterDefinitions)
  1819	        {
  1820	            var filterDefinitionsToApply = filterDefinitions.Where(x => FilterDefinitions.All(y => y.Id != x.Id)).ToArray();
  1821	            FilterDefinitions.AddRange(filterDefinitionsToApply);
  1822	
  1823	            await InvokeServerLoadFunc();
  1824	            GroupItems();
  1825	            await NotifyFilterChangedAsync();
  1826	
  1827	            if (!HasServerData)
  1828	            {
  1829	                StateHasChanged();
  1830	            }
  1831	        }
  1832	
  1833	        private async Task ClearFilterFromSimpleModeAsync(IFilterDefinition<T> filterDefinition)
  1834	        {
  1835	            await RemoveFilterAsync(filterDefinition.Id);
  1836	
  1837	            if (!HasServerData)
  1838	            {
  1839	                StateHasChanged();
  1840	            }
  1841	        }
  1842	
  1843	        private async Task ClearFiltersFromSimpleModeAsync(IEnumerable<IFilterDefinition<T>> filterDefinitions)
  1844	        {
  1845	            FilterDefinitions.RemoveAll(x => filterDefinitions.Any(y => y.Id == x.Id));
  1846	
  1847	            await InvokeServerLoadFunc();
  1848	            GroupItems();
  1849	            await NotifyFilterChangedAsync();
  1850	
  1851	            if (!HasServerData)
  1852	            {
  1853	                StateHasChanged();
  1854	            }
  1855	        }

  1874	        /// <summary>

  1876	        /// </summary>

  1878	        {
  1879	            var column = RenderedColumns.FirstOrDefault(x => x.filterable);
  1880	            var filterDefinition = CreateFilterDefinitionInstance();
  1881	            filterDefinition.Id = Guid.NewGuid();
  1882	            filterDefinition.Title = column?.Title;
  1883	            filterDefinition.Column = column;

  1885	            _filtersMenuVisible = true;
  1886	            StateHasChanged();
  1887	        }

  1893	        }

  1895	        /// <summary>
  1896	        /// Closes the filter UI owned by this data grid.
  1897	        /// </summary>

  1899	        /// This method closes the filter panel shown by <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}"/>, such as the panel used by <see cref="DataGridFilterMode.Simple"/>.
  1900	        /// Incomplete filters which still require a value are removed as part of closing the panel.
  1901	        /// </remarks>

  1903	        {
  1904	            _filtersMenuVisible = false;
  1905	            CleanupIncompleteFilters();
  1906	            StateHasChanged();
  1907	            return Task.CompletedTask;
  1908	        }

  1910	        /// <summary>
  1911	        /// Removes all filters from all columns.
  1912	        /// </summary>
  1913	        public async Task ClearFiltersAsync()
  1914	        {
  1915	            FilterDefinitions.ForEach(x => x.Value = null);
  1916	            FilterDefinitions.Clear();
  1917	            await InvokeServerLoadFunc();
  1918	            await NotifyFilterChangedAsync();
  1919	        }
  1920	
  1921	        /// <summary>
  1922	        /// Adds the specified filter to the list of filters.
  1923	        /// </summary>
  1924	        /// <param name="definition">The filter to add.</param>
  1925	        public async Task AddFilterAsync(IFilterDefinition<T> definition)
  1926	        {
  1927	            if (FilterDefinitions.All(x => x.Id != definition.Id))
  1928	            {
  1929	                FilterDefinitions.Add(definition);
  1930	            }
  1931	            _filtersMenuVisible = true;
  1932	            await InvokeServerLoadFunc();
  1933	            await NotifyFilterChangedAsync();
  1934	            if (!HasServerData) StateHasChanged();
  1935	        }
  1936	
  1937	        internal async Task RemoveFilterAsync(Guid? id)
  1938	        {
  1939	            var index = FilterDefinitions.FindIndex(x => x.Id == id);
  1940	            if (index == -1)
  1941	            {
  1942	                return;
  1943	            }
  1944	
  1945	            FilterDefinitions[index].Value = null;
  1946	            FilterDefinitions.RemoveAt(index);
  1947	            await InvokeServerLoadFunc();
  1948	            GroupItems();
  1949	            await NotifyFilterChangedAsync();
  1950	        }
  1951	
  1952	        private Task NotifyFilterChangedAsync() => FilterChanged.InvokeAsync(FilterDefinitions.AsReadOnly());
  1953	
  1954	        internal async Task SetSelectedItemAsync(bool value, T item)
  1955	        {
  1956	            Debug.Assert(item is not null);
  1957	            var selectColumn = RenderedColumns.OfType<SelectColumn<T>>().FirstOrDefault();
  1958	
  1959	            if (selectColumn?.DisabledFunc?.Invoke(item) is true)
  1960	                return; // Do not change selection if the item is disabled
  1961	
  1962	            if (value)
  1963	            {
  1964	                if (!MultiSelection)
  1965	                {
  1966	                    Selection.Clear();
  1967	                }
  1968	
  1969	                Selection.Add(item);
  1970	                await _selectedItemState.SetValueAsync(item);
  1971	            }
  1972	            else
  1973	            {
  1974	                Selection.Remove(item);
  1975	                if (Comparer != null)
  1976	                {
  1977	                    if (Comparer.Equals(item, _selectedItemState.Value))
  1978	                    {
  1979	                        await _selectedItemState.SetValueAsync(default);
  1980	                    }
  1981	                }
  1982	                else
  1983	                {
  1984	                    if (item.Equals(_selectedItemState.Value))
  1985	                    {
  1986	                        await _selectedItemState.SetValueAsync(default);
  1987	                    }
  1988	                }
  1989	            }
  1990	
  1991	            // Create new HashSet instance to ensure ParameterState's comparer detects changes
  1992	            await _selectedItemsState.SetValueAsync(new HashSet<T>(Selection, Comparer));
  1993	            await InvokeAsync(() => SelectedItemsChangedEvent?.Invoke(Selection));
  1994	
  1995	            await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
  1996	        }
  1997	
  1998	        /// <summary>
  1999	        /// Set the currently selected item in the data grid.
  2000	        /// </summary>
  2001	        /// <param name="item">The item to select.</param>
  2002	        /// <remarks>
  2003	        /// When <see cref="MultiSelection"/> is <c>true</c> and <see cref="SelectOnRowClick"/> is <c>true</c>, the <see cref="SelectedItems"/> are updated.  The <see cref="SelectedItem"/> is also updated.
  2004	        /// </remarks>
  2005	        public Task SetSelectedItemAsync(T item)
  2006	        {
  2007	            if (!SelectOnRowClick)
  2008	            {
  2009	                return Task.CompletedTask;
  2010	            }
  2011	
  2012	            var isSelected = Selection.Contains(item);
  2013	            return SetSelectedItemAsync(!isSelected, item);
  2014	        }
  2015	
  2016	        internal async Task SetSelectAllAsync(bool value)
  2017	        {
  2018	            // nothing should happen if multiselection is false
  2019	            if (!MultiSelection)
  2020	                return;
  2021	
  2022	            Selection.Clear(); // Clear selection first, regardless of selecting or unselecting all.
  2023	
  2024	            if (value) // Logic for selecting all
  2025	            {
  2026	                var itemsToSelect = HasServerData ? ServerItems : FilteredItems;
  2027	
  2028	                var selectColumn = RenderedColumns.OfType<SelectColumn<T>>().FirstOrDefault();
  2029	                if (selectColumn?.DisabledFunc != null)
  2030	                {
  2031	                    // Filter out disabled items before adding to selection
  2032	                    itemsToSelect = itemsToSelect.Where(item => !selectColumn.DisabledFunc(item));
  2033	                }
  2034	
  2035	                Selection.UnionWith(itemsToSelect);
  2036	            }
  2037	
  2038	            // Create new HashSet instance to ensure ParameterState's comparer detects changes
  2039	            await InvokeAsync(() => _selectedItemsState.SetValueAsync(new HashSet<T>(Selection, Comparer)));
  2040	            await InvokeAsync(() => SelectedItemsChangedEvent?.Invoke(Selection));
  2041	            await InvokeAsync(() => SelectedAllItemsChangedEvent?.Invoke(value));
  2042	
  2043	            await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
  2044	        }
  2045	
  2046	        internal IEnumerable<T> Sort(IEnumerable<T> items)
  2047	        {
  2048	            if (!items.Any())
  2049	                return items;
  2050	
  2051	            if (null == SortDefinitions || 0 == SortDefinitions.Count)
  2052	                return items;
  2053	
  2054	            IOrderedEnumerable<T>? orderedEnumerable = null;
  2055	
  2056	            foreach (var sortDefinition in SortDefinitions.Values.Where(sd => sd.SortFunc != null).OrderBy(sd => sd.Index))
  2057	            {
  2058	                Debug.Assert(sortDefinition.SortFunc is not null);
  2059	                if (null == orderedEnumerable)
  2060	                    orderedEnumerable = sortDefinition.Descending ? items.OrderByDescending(item => sortDefinition.SortFunc(item), sortDefinition.Comparer)
  2061	                        : items.OrderBy(item => sortDefinition.SortFunc(item), sortDefinition.Comparer);
  2062	                else
  2063	                    orderedEnumerable = sortDefinition.Descending ? orderedEnumerable.ThenByDescending(item => sortDefinition.SortFunc(item), sortDefinition.Comparer)
  2064	                        : orderedEnumerable.ThenBy(item => sortDefinition.SortFunc(item), sortDefinition.Comparer);
  2065	            }
  2066	
  2067	            return orderedEnumerable ?? items;
  2068	        }
  2069	
  2070	        internal void ClearEditingItem()
  2071	        {
  2072	            _editingItem = default;
  2073	            _editingSourceItem = default;
  2074	        }
  2075	
  2076	        /// <summary>
  2077	        /// This method notifies the consumer that changes to the data have been committed
  2078	        /// and what those changes are. This variation of the method is only used by the Cell
  2079	        /// when the EditMode is set to cell.
  2080	        /// </summary>
  2081	        /// <param name="item"></param>
  2082	        /// <returns></returns>
  2083	        internal async Task CommitItemChangesAsync(T item)
  2084	        {
  2085	            // Here, we need to validate at the cellular level...
  2086	            if (CommittedItemChanges != null)
  2087	                _ = await CommittedItemChanges(item); // ignore return value in cell edit mode
  2088	
  2089	            await CommittedItemChanged.InvokeAsync(item);
  2090	        }
  2091	
  2092	        /// <summary>
  2093	        /// This method notifies the consumer that changes to the data have been committed
  2094	        /// and what those changes are. This variation of the method is used when the EditMode
  2095	        /// is anything but Cell since the _editingItem is used.
  2096	        /// </summary>
  2097	        /// <returns></returns>
  2098	        internal async Task CommitItemChangesAsync()
  2099	        {
  2100	            Debug.Assert(_editingItem is not null);
  2101	            Debug.Assert(_editForm is not null);
  2102	            await _editForm.ValidateAsync();
  2103	            if (!_editForm.IsValid)
  2104	            {
  2105	                return;
  2106	            }
  2107	
  2108	            if (_editingSourceItem != null)
  2109	            {
  2110	                if (CommittedItemChanges != null)
  2111	                {
  2112	                    var closeBehavior = await CommittedItemChanges(_editingItem);
  2113	
  2114	                    if (closeBehavior == DataGridEditFormAction.KeepOpen)
  2115	                        return;
  2116	                }
  2117	
  2118	                foreach (var property in _properties.Where(p => p.CanWrite))
  2119	                    property.SetValue(_editingSourceItem, property.GetValue(_editingItem));
  2120	
  2121	                await CommittedItemChanged.InvokeAsync(_editingSourceItem);
  2122	
  2123	                ClearEditingItem();
  2124	                _isEditFormOpen = false;
  2125	            }
  2126	        }
  2127	
  2128	        internal async Task OnRowClickedAsync(MouseEventArgs args, T item, int rowIndex)
  2129	        {
  2130	            await RowClick.InvokeAsync(new DataGridRowClickEventArgs<T>(args, item, rowIndex));
  2131	
  2132	            if (EditMode != DataGridEditMode.Cell && EditTrigger == DataGridEditTrigger.OnRowClick)
  2133	                await SetEditingItemAsync(item);
  2134	
  2135	            await SetSelectedItemAsync(item);
  2136	        }

  2143	        /// <summary>
  2144	        /// Gets the total count of filtered items in the data grid.
  2145	        /// </summary>
  2146	        /// <returns>
  2147	        /// The number of items remaining after applying filters.  When <see cref="ServerData"/> is in use, the <see cref="GridData{T}.TotalItems"/> value is returned.
  2148	        /// </returns>
  2149	        public int GetFilteredItemsCount()
  2150	        {
  2151	            if (HasServerData)
  2152	                return _serverData.TotalItems;
  2153	            return FilteredItems.Count();
  2154	        }
  2155	
  2156	        /// <summary>
  2157	        /// Navigates to a page when this grid has a <see cref="MudDataGridPager{T}"/>.
  2158	        /// </summary>
  2159	        /// <param name="page">The page to navigate to.</param>
  2160	        public void NavigateTo(Page page)
  2161	        {
  2162	            CurrentPage = page switch
  2163	            {
  2164	                Page.First => 0,
  2165	                Page.Last => Math.Max(0, numPages - 1),
  2166	                Page.Next => Math.Min(numPages - 1, CurrentPage + 1),
  2167	                Page.Previous => Math.Max(0, CurrentPage - 1),
  2168	                _ => CurrentPage
  2169	            };
  2170	
  2171	            GroupItems();
  2172	        }
  2173	
  2174	        /// <summary>
  2175	        /// Sets the <see cref="RowsPerPage"/> when this grid contains a <see cref="MudDataGridPager{T}"/>.
  2176	        /// </summary>
  2177	        /// <param name="size">The new page size.</param>
  2178	        public Task SetRowsPerPageAsync(int size) => SetRowsPerPageAsync(size, true);
  2179	
  2180	        /// <summary>
  2181	        /// Sets the <see cref="RowsPerPage"/> when this grid contains a <see cref="MudDataGridPager{T}"/>.
  2182	        /// </summary>
  2183	        /// <param name="size">The new page size.</param>
  2184	        /// <param name="resetPage">When <c>true</c>, resets <see cref="CurrentPage"/> to 0.</param>
  2185	        public async Task SetRowsPerPageAsync(int size, bool resetPage)
  2186	        {
  2187	            if (_rowsPerPage == size)
  2188	                return;
  2189	
  2190	            _rowsPerPage = size;
  2191	
  2192	            if (resetPage)
  2193	            {
  2194	                var currentPageHasChanged = _currentPage != 0;
  2195	                _currentPage = 0;
  2196	                if (currentPageHasChanged)
  2197	                    await CurrentPageChanged.InvokeAsync(_currentPage);
  2198	            }
  2199	
  2200	            await RowsPerPageChanged.InvokeAsync(_rowsPerPage.Value);
  2201	
  2202	            StateHasChanged();
  2203	
  2204	            if (_isFirstRendered)
  2205	                await InvokeAsync(InvokeServerLoadFunc);
  2206	        }
  2207	
  2208	        /// <summary>
  2209	        /// Replaces the sorting behavior for a field.
  2210	        /// </summary>
  2211	        /// <param name="field">The field to sort.</param>
  2212	        /// <param name="direction">The direction to sort results.</param>
  2213	        /// <param name="sortFunc">The function which sorts results.</param>
  2214	        /// <param name="comparer">The comparer used for custom comparisons.</param>
  2215	        public async Task SetSortAsync(string field, SortDirection direction, Func<T, object?> sortFunc, IComparer<object?>? comparer = null)
  2216	        {
  2217	            var removedSortDefinitions = new HashSet<string>(SortDefinitions.Keys);
  2218	            SortDefinitions.Clear();
  2219	
  2220	            var newDefinition = new SortDefinition<T>(field, direction == SortDirection.Descending, 0, sortFunc, comparer);
  2221	            SortDefinitions[field] = newDefinition;
  2222	
  2223	            // In case sort is just updated make sure to not mark the field as removed
  2224	            removedSortDefinitions.Remove(field);
  2225	
  2226	            await InvokeSortUpdates(SortDefinitions, removedSortDefinitions);
  2227	        }
  2228	
  2229	        /// <summary>
  2230	        /// Adds or replaces a sort behavior depending on the <see cref="SortMode"/>.
  2231	        /// </summary>
  2232	        /// <param name="field">The field to sort.</param>
  2233	        /// <param name="direction">The direction to sort results.</param>
  2234	        /// <param name="sortFunc">The function which sorts results.</param>
  2235	        /// <param name="comparer">The comparer used for custom comparisons.</param>
  2236	        /// <remarks>
  2237	        /// When the <see cref="SortMode"/> is <see cref="SortMode.Single"/>, this method replaces the sort column.  Otherwise, this sort is appended to any existing sort column.
  2238	        /// </remarks>
  2239	        public async Task ExtendSortAsync(string field, SortDirection direction, Func<T, object?> sortFunc, IComparer<object?>? comparer = null)
  2240	        {
  2241	            // If SortMode is not multiple, use the default set approach and don't extend.
  2242	            if (SortMode != SortMode.Multiple)
  2243	            {
  2244	                await SetSortAsync(field, direction, sortFunc, comparer);
  2245	                return;
  2246	            }
  2247	
  2248	            // in case it already exists, just update the current entry
  2249	            if (SortDefinitions.TryGetValue(field, out var sortDefinition))
  2250	                SortDefinitions[field] = sortDefinition with { Descending = direction == SortDirection.Descending, SortFunc = sortFunc, Comparer = comparer };
  2251	            else
  2252	            {
  2253	                var newDefinition = new SortDefinition<T>(field, direction == SortDirection.Descending, SortDefinitions.Count, sortFunc, comparer);
  2254	                SortDefinitions[field] = newDefinition;

  2264	        public async Task RemoveSortAsync(string? field)

  2266	            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(field) && SortDefinitions.TryGetValue(field, out var definition))
  2267	            {

  2269	                foreach (var defToUpdate in SortDefinitions.Where(kvp => kvp.Value.Index > definition.Index).ToList())

  2271

  2273	            }
  2274	        }

  2298	        private void VirtualItemsProviderInitialize()
  2299	        {
  2300	            if (VirtualItemsProvider != null || VirtualizeServerData == null)
  2301	            {
  2302	                return;
  2303	            }
  2304

  2306	            {
  2307	                var stateFunc = (int startIndex, int count) => new GridStateVirtualize<T>
  2308	                {
  2309	                    StartIndex = startIndex,
  2310	                    Count = count,
  2311	                    SortDefinitions = SortDefinitions.Values.OrderBy(sd => sd.Index).ToList(),
  2312	                    // Additional ToList() here to decouple clients from internal list avoiding runtime issues
  2313	                    FilterDefinitions = FilterDefinitions.ToList()
  2314	                };
  2315

  2317	                    stateFunc(request.StartIndex, request.Count),
  2318	                    request.CancellationToken
  2319	                );
  2320	
  2321	                //do not reset cache, the current chunk load has been cancelled, we wait for the final load
  2322	                if (!request.CancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)
  2323	                {

  2325	                }

  2328	                    _serverData.Items.Select((item, index) => new IndexBag<T>(request.StartIndex + index, item)),
  2329	                    _serverData.TotalItems);
  2330	            };
  2331	        }

   285	                await DataGrid.ExpandAllHierarchy();
   286	            }
   287	        }
   288	
   289	        internal string GetGroupIcon()
   290	        {
   291	            return DataGrid?.GetGroupIcon(Expanded, RightToLeft) ?? string.Empty;
   292	        }
   293	
   294	        /// <summary>
   295	        /// This is triggered by the DataGrid when a sort is applied
   296	        /// e.g. from another HeaderCell.
   297	        /// </summary>
   298	        /// <param name="activeSorts">The active sorts.</param>
   299	        /// <param name="removedSorts">The removed sorts.</param>
   300	        private void OnGridSortChanged(Dictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> activeSorts, HashSet<string>? removedSorts)
   301	        {
   302	            if (Column == null || (Column.Sortable.HasValue && !Column.Sortable.Value) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Column.PropertyName))
   303	                return;
   304	
   305	            if (null != removedSorts && removedSorts.Contains(Column.PropertyName))
   306	            {
   307	                MarkAsUnsorted();
   308	            }
   309	            else if (activeSorts.TryGetValue(Column.PropertyName, out var sortDefinition))
   310	            {
   311	                Column.SortIndex = sortDefinition.Index;
   312	            }
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        private void OnSelectedAllItemsChanged(bool value)
   316	        {
   317	            _selected = value;
   318	            StateHasChanged();
   319	        }
   320	
   321	        private void OnSelectedItemsChanged(HashSet<T> items)
   322	        {
   323	            Debug.Assert(DataGrid is not null);
   324	            _selected = items.Count == DataGrid.GetFilteredItemsCount();
   325	            StateHasChanged();
   326	        }
   327	
   328	        private async Task OnResizerPointerDown(PointerEventArgs args)
   329	        {
   330	            Debug.Assert(DataGrid is not null);
   331	            if (!resizable)
   332	                return;
   333	
   334	            if (args.Detail > 1) // Double click clears the width, hence setting it to minimum size.
   335	            {
   336	                Width = null;
   337	                return;
   338	            }
   339	
   340	            // Start resize using simplified approach
   341	            _resizeStartX = args.ClientX;
   342	            _resizeStartWidth = await GetCurrentCellWidth();
   343	
   344	            if (DataGrid.ColumnResizeMode == ResizeMode.Column && Column is not null)
   345	            {
   346	                // Find next resizable column
   347	                var columns = DataGrid.RenderedColumns;
   348	                var currentIndex = columns.IndexOf(Column);
   349	                var nextIndex = currentIndex + (RightToLeft ? -1 : 1);

// MudBlazor licenses this file to you under the MIT license.
// See the LICENSE file in the project root for more information.

using System.Collections.Generic;

namespace MudBlazor
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Represents the information related to a <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}.SortChanged"/> event.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">The item managed by the <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}"/>.</typeparam>
    public class DataGridSortChangedEventArgs<T>
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// The current active sort definitions.
        /// </summary>
        public IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> ActiveSortDefinitions { get; }

        /// <summary>
        /// The sort definitions that were removed, or <c>null</c> if no sorts were removed.
        /// </summary>
        public IReadOnlySet<string>? RemovedSortDefinitions { get; }

        /// <summary>
        /// Creates a new instance of <see cref="DataGridSortChangedEventArgs{T}"/>.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="activeSortDefinitions">The current active sort definitions.</param>
        /// <param name="removedSortDefinitions">The sort definitions that were removed.</param>
        public DataGridSortChangedEventArgs(
            IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> activeSortDefinitions,
            IReadOnlySet<string>? removedSortDefinitions)
        {
            ActiveSortDefinitions = activeSortDefinitions;
            RemovedSortDefinitions = removedSortDefinitions;
        }
    }
}'

﻿// Copyright (c) MudBlazor 2021
// MudBlazor licenses this file to you under the MIT license.
// See the LICENSE file in the project root for more information.

using System.Collections.Generic;

namespace MudBlazor
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Represents the information related to a <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}.SortChanged"/> event.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">The item managed by the <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}"/>.</typeparam>
    public class DataGridSortChangedEventArgs<T>
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// The current active sort definitions.
        /// </summary>
        public IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> ActiveSortDefinitions { get; }

        /// <summary>
        /// The sort definitions that were removed, or <c>null</c> if no sorts were removed.
        /// </summary>
        public IReadOnlySet<string>? RemovedSortDefinitions { get; }

        /// <summary>
        /// Creates a new instance of <see cref="DataGridSortChangedEventArgs{T}"/>.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="activeSortDefinitions">The current active sort definitions.</param>
        /// <param name="removedSortDefinitions">The sort definitions that were removed.</param>
        public DataGridSortChangedEventArgs(
            IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> activeSortDefinitions,
            IReadOnlySet<string>? removedSortDefinitions)
        {
            ActiveSortDefinitions = activeSortDefinitions;
            RemovedSortDefinitions = removedSortDefinitions;
        }
    }
}

2. **Event firing**: The event is fired in `InvokeSortUpdates`, which is called from:
   - `SetSortAsync` - when a single sort is set
   - `ExtendSortAsync` - when a sort is added/extended
   - `RemoveSortAsync` - when a sort is removed
   - `ClearCurrentSortings` - when all sorts are cleared (e.g., when SortMode changes)

   - `ActiveSortDefinitions` (IReadOnlyDictionary) - the current active sorts
   - `RemovedSortDefinitions` (IReadOnlySet<string>) - the sorts that were removed

=== New file ===
﻿// Copyright (c) MudBlazor 2021
// MudBlazor licenses this file to you under the MIT license.
// See the LICENSE file in the project root for more information.

using System.Collections.Generic;

namespace MudBlazor
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Represents the information related to a <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}.SortChanged"/> event.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">The item managed by the <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}"/>.</typeparam>
    public class DataGridSortChangedEventArgs<T>
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// The current active sort definitions.
        /// </summary>
        public IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> ActiveSortDefinitions { get; }

        /// <summary>
        /// The sort definitions that were removed, or <c>null</c> if no sorts were removed.
        /// </summary>
        public IReadOnlySet<string>? RemovedSortDefinitions { get; }

        /// <summary>
        /// Creates a new instance of <see cref="DataGridSortChangedEventArgs{T}"/>.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="activeSortDefinitions">The current active sort definitions.</param>
        /// <param name="removedSortDefinitions">The sort definitions that were removed.</param>
        public DataGridSortChangedEventArgs(
            IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> activeSortDefinitions,
            IReadOnlySet<string>? removedSortDefinitions)
        {
            ActiveSortDefinitions = activeSortDefinitions;
            RemovedSortDefinitions = removedSortDefinitions;
        }
    }
}

+    /// </summary>
+    /// <typeparam name="T">The item managed by the <see cref="MudDataGrid{T}"/>.</typeparam>
+    public class DataGridSortChangedEventArgs<T>
+    {
+        /// <summary>
+        /// The current active sort definitions.
+        /// </summary>
+        public IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> ActiveSortDefinitions { get; }
+
+        /// <summary>
+        /// The sort definitions that were removed, or <c>null</c> if no sorts were removed.
+        /// </summary>
+        public IReadOnlySet<string>? RemovedSortDefinitions { get; }
+

+        /// Creates a new instance of <see cref="DataGridSortChangedEventArgs{T}"/>.
+        /// </summary>
+        /// <param name="activeSortDefinitions">The current active sort definitions.</param>
+        /// <param name="removedSortDefinitions">The sort definitions that were removed.</param>
+        public DataGridSortChangedEventArgs(
+            IReadOnlyDictionary<string, SortDefinition<T>> activeSortDefinitions,
+            IReadOnlySet<string>? removedSortDefinitions)
+        {
+            ActiveSortDefinitions = activeSortDefinitions;
+            RemovedSortDefinitions = removedSortDefinitions;
+        }
+    }
+}
